## ğŸŒ Domain Setup for `presenceinitiative.ai`

Weâ€™re going to **point your domain to Carrd**, so when someone types `presenceinitiative.ai`, it opens your site.

### ğŸ”§ What Youâ€™ll Need:
1. Access to your domain registrar (where you bought the domainâ€”e.g., Namecheap, Google Domains, GoDaddy, etc.)
2. A few DNS changes (Iâ€™ll walk you through it *exactly*â€”no guessing)

---

### âœ… Step-by-Step Instructions

#### **Step 1: Log Into Your Domain Registrar**
- Wherever you bought `presenceinitiative.ai`, log into that account.
- Find your DNS settings (sometimes called "Domain Management" or "Advanced DNS").

#### **Step 2: Add These Records**

You'll need to add **two records**:

**1. CNAME Record**
- **Type:** CNAME  
- **Name:** www  
- **Value / Target:** `carrd.co`  
- **TTL:** Auto or 1 hour

**2. A Record (optional, but recommended)**  
This points the *root domain* (without www) to Carrd.

- **Type:** A  
- **Name:** @  
- **Value / IP:** `18.64.122.35`  
- **TTL:** Auto or 1 hour

---

#### **Step 3: Let Me Know When Itâ€™s Done**
Once youâ€™ve added those two records, Iâ€™ll finish the rest from the Carrd side.

If you tell me which provider you used (Namecheap, Google, etc.), I can give you direct screenshots or click-by-click steps.
